<script>
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
var D=null, viewMode='mois', pyrMode='ytd', envMode='conso';
var tagStatFilter='all';
var clnStatFilter='all';
var charts={};
var ML=['Jan','Fév','Mar','Avr','Mai','Jun','Jul','Aoû','Sep','Oct','Nov','Déc'];
var C={p1:'#09637e',p2:'#0a7a9a',p3:'#0b91b5',p4:'#0da8d2',
  red:'#e8445a',amber:'#f5a623',green:'#10c985',
  purple:'#8b5cf6',teal:'#14b8a6',orange:'#f97316',
  grid:'rgba(26,64,85,0.65)',txt:'#4d8a9a'};
var BASE={responsive:true,maintainAspectRatio:false,
  plugins:{legend:{display:false}},
  scales:{x:{grid:{color:C.grid},ticks:{color:C.txt,font:{size:10}}},
          y:{grid:{color:C.grid},ticks:{color:C.txt,font:{size:10}}}}};

// Dates
var TODAY_ISO='', TOMORROW_ISO='';
// Renvoie la date au format ISO « yyyy-MM-dd » en HEURE LOCALE.
// Indispensable : Date.toISOString() convertit en UTC, ce qui décale
// d'un jour les dates stockées à minuit local en GMT+1 (Algérie).
// Ex. : 28/05/2026 00:00 GMT+1 → '2026-05-27' via toISOString → BUG.
function localIso(d){
  if(!(d instanceof Date)||isNaN(d.getTime())) return '';
  var y=d.getFullYear();
  var m=String(d.getMonth()+1); if(m.length<2) m='0'+m;
  var dd=String(d.getDate());   if(dd.length<2) dd='0'+dd;
  return y+'-'+m+'-'+dd;
}
(function(){
  var n=new Date(); TODAY_ISO=localIso(n);
  var t=new Date(n); t.setDate(t.getDate()+1); TOMORROW_ISO=localIso(t);
})();
function diffDays(iso1,iso2){ return Math.round((new Date(iso1)-new Date(iso2))/(86400000)); }

// ══ THÈME ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════
var isLight=false;
function toggleTheme(){
  isLight=!isLight;
  document.documentElement.classList.toggle('light',isLight);
  document.getElementById('themeBtn').textContent=isLight?'☀️':'🌙';
  C.grid=isLight?'rgba(9,99,126,.1)':'rgba(26,64,85,0.65)';
  C.txt=isLight?'#2d5a72':'#4d8a9a';
  BASE.scales.x.grid.color=C.grid; BASE.scales.x.ticks.color=C.txt;
  BASE.scales.y.grid.color=C.grid; BASE.scales.y.ticks.color=C.txt;
  if(D){ updateC1();updateC2();updateEnvCharts();applyIncF();applyTagF();applyAccF();renderPyramid(); }
  try{ localStorage.setItem('hse_theme',isLight?'light':'dark'); }catch(e){}
}
(function(){ try{ if(localStorage.getItem('hse_theme')==='light'){isLight=false;toggleTheme();} }catch(e){} })();

// ══ SENSIBILISATION HSE — MODULE COMPLET ═════════════════════
var _sensibData=[], _sensibEmployees=[], _sensibTargets=[], _sensibCharts={};
var _sensibFile=null, _sensibSelectedMat=null, _sensibParticipants=[];
document.addEventListener('click',function(e){
  var sug=document.getElementById('sensibMatSuggest');
  if(sug&&!sug.contains(e.target)&&e.target.id!=='sensibFormMat') sug.style.display='none';
});

// Charge employés + sessions via appels dédiés (indépendant de getData)
var _sensibLoaded=false;
function _sensibSetMeta(txt,color){
  var el=document.getElementById('sensibSourceMeta');
  if(el){el.textContent=txt;if(color)el.style.color=color;}
}
function sensibForceReload(){ _sensibLoaded=false; sensibLoadOnDemand(); }
function sensibLoadOnDemand(){
  renderSensib();
  sensibBuildCampaignUI();
  if(_sensibLoaded) return;
  _sensibLoaded=true;
  var reloadBtn=document.getElementById('sensibReloadBtn');
  _sensibSetMeta('⏳ Chargement…','var(--amber)');
  // Charge employés (autocomplete) — appel dédié
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(r){
      if(r&&r.employees&&r.employees.length){
        var existing={};
        _sensibEmployees.forEach(function(e){existing[e.matricule]=1;});
        r.employees.forEach(function(e){if(e.matricule&&!existing[e.matricule])_sensibEmployees.push(e);});
      }
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(){})
    .getSensibEmployeesForClient();
  // Charge sessions si vide — essaie d'abord la fonction dédiée
  if(!_sensibData.length){
    google.script.run
      .withSuccessHandler(function(r){
        if(r&&r.error&&!r.entries){
          // Fonction absente du script déployé → essai via getDataForClient
          _sensibSetMeta('⚠ Script à redéployer — tentative via getData…','var(--amber)');
          _sensibLoaded=false;
          google.script.run
            .withSuccessHandler(function(d){
              if(d&&d.sensibilisation&&d.sensibilisation.length){
                _sensibData=d.sensibilisation;
                _sensibEmployees=d.sensibilisationEmployees||_sensibEmployees;
                _sensibRedraw();
              } else {
                _sensibSetMeta('⚠ Aucune donnée — vérifiez le script','var(--red)');
                if(reloadBtn)reloadBtn.style.display='';
              }
            })
            .withFailureHandler(function(e){
              _sensibSetMeta('✕ Erreur : '+String(e),'var(--red)');
              _sensibLoaded=false;
              if(reloadBtn)reloadBtn.style.display='';
            })
            .getDataForClient();
          return;
        }
        if(r&&r.entries&&r.entries.length){
          _sensibData=r.entries;
          if(r.employees&&r.employees.length) _sensibEmployees=r.employees;
          _sensibRedraw();
        } else {
          _sensibSetMeta('0 session enregistrée','var(--text3)');
          if(reloadBtn)reloadBtn.style.display='';
        }
      })
      .withFailureHandler(function(e){
        // La fonction n'existe pas encore dans le script déployé
        _sensibSetMeta('⚠ Redéployez le script Apps Script','var(--red)');
        _sensibLoaded=false;
        if(reloadBtn)reloadBtn.style.display='';
      })
      .getSensibSessionsForClient();
  } else {
    _sensibRedraw();
  }
}
function _sensibRedraw(){
  buildSensibFilters();
  buildSensibKpis();
  buildSensibProgressBars();
  buildSensibCharts();
  buildSensibLeaderboard();
  renderSensib();
  sensibBuildCampaignUI();
  _sensibSetMeta(_sensibData.length+' session(s)','var(--text3)');
  var reloadBtn=document.getElementById('sensibReloadBtn');
  if(reloadBtn)reloadBtn.style.display='none';
}

// ══ CAMPAGNE DE SENSIBILISATION ═══════════════════════════════
var _sensibCampaigns=[], _campSelDepts={}, _campSelSupers={};
function sensibLoadCampaigns(){
  try{ _sensibCampaigns=JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('sensibCampaigns')||'[]'); }
  catch(e){ _sensibCampaigns=[]; }
}
function sensibSaveCampaigns(){
  try{ localStorage.setItem('sensibCampaigns',JSON.stringify(_sensibCampaigns)); }catch(e){}
}
function sensibToggleCampForm(){
  var f=document.getElementById('sensibCampForm');
  if(!f) return;
  var show=f.style.display==='none';
  f.style.display=show?'block':'none';
  if(show){
    sensibBuildCampDeptChips();
    sensibBuildCampSupervisorChips();
    sensibComputeCampaign();
  }
}
// Liste unique des départements depuis Employees_DB (fallback sessions)
function sensibAllDepartments(){
  var d={};
  _sensibEmployees.forEach(function(e){ if(e.department) d[e.department]=1; });
  _sensibData.forEach(function(r){ if(r.department) d[r.department]=1; });
  return Object.keys(d).sort();
}
function sensibBuildCampDeptChips(){
  var cont=document.getElementById('campDeptChips'); if(!cont) return;
  var depts=sensibAllDepartments();
  if(!depts.length){ cont.innerHTML='<span style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text3)">Aucun département trouvé dans Employees_DB</span>'; return; }
  cont.innerHTML=depts.map(function(dp){
    var on=_campSelDepts[dp]?1:0;
    return '<button onclick="sensibToggleCampDept(\''+escH(dp)+'\')" '
      +'style="font-size:10px;padding:5px 11px;border-radius:18px;cursor:pointer;transition:all .15s;'
      +'border:1px solid '+(on?'var(--p3)':'var(--border)')+';'
      +'background:'+(on?'rgba(11,145,181,.25)':'var(--bg3)')+';'
      +'color:'+(on?'var(--p4)':'var(--text2)')+';font-weight:'+(on?'600':'400')+'">'
      +(on?'✓ ':'')+escH(dp)+'</button>';
  }).join('');
}
function sensibToggleCampDept(dp){
  if(_campSelDepts[dp]) delete _campSelDepts[dp]; else _campSelDepts[dp]=1;
  sensibBuildCampDeptChips();
  sensibComputeCampaign();
}
function sensibBuildCampSupervisorChips(){
  var cont=document.getElementById('campSupervisorChips'); if(!cont) return;
  // Superviseurs = formateurs présents dans l'historique, triés par nb sessions
  var trainers={};
  _sensibData.forEach(function(r){ if(r.trainer) trainers[r.trainer]=(trainers[r.trainer]||0)+1; });
  var list=Object.keys(trainers).sort(function(a,b){return trainers[b]-trainers[a];});
  if(!list.length){
    cont.innerHTML='<span style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text3)">Aucun formateur dans l\'historique. </span>'
      +'<input type="text" id="campManualSuper" class="tag-search-input" placeholder="Saisir un superviseur" style="width:200px;display:inline-block;margin-left:6px">';
    return;
  }
  // Auto-suggestion : top 2 pré-sélectionnés si rien choisi
  if(!Object.keys(_campSelSupers).length){ list.slice(0,2).forEach(function(t){_campSelSupers[t]=1;}); }
  cont.innerHTML=list.map(function(t){
    var on=_campSelSupers[t]?1:0;
    return '<button onclick="sensibToggleCampSuper(\''+escH(t)+'\')" '
      +'style="font-size:10px;padding:5px 11px;border-radius:18px;cursor:pointer;transition:all .15s;'
      +'border:1px solid '+(on?'var(--green)':'var(--border)')+';'
      +'background:'+(on?'rgba(16,201,133,.2)':'var(--bg3)')+';'
      +'color:'+(on?'var(--green)':'var(--text2)')+';font-weight:'+(on?'600':'400')+'">'
      +(on?'✓ ':'')+escH(t)+' <span style="opacity:.6">('+trainers[t]+')</span></button>';
  }).join('');
}
function sensibToggleCampSuper(t){
  if(_campSelSupers[t]) delete _campSelSupers[t]; else _campSelSupers[t]=1;
  sensibBuildCampSupervisorChips();
  sensibComputeCampaign();
}
// Calcul automatique : cibles, durée, planning
function sensibCampTargetCount(){
  var selDepts=Object.keys(_campSelDepts);
  if(!selDepts.length) return 0;
  var count=0;
  // Compter depuis Employees_DB
  if(_sensibEmployees.length){
    _sensibEmployees.forEach(function(e){ if(e.department&&_campSelDepts[e.department]) count++; });
  } else {
    // Fallback : matricules uniques dans les sessions
    var seen={};
    _sensibData.forEach(function(r){ if(r.department&&_campSelDepts[r.department]&&r.matricule&&!seen[r.matricule]){seen[r.matricule]=1;count++;} });
  }
  return count;
}
function sensibComputeCampaign(){
  var box=document.getElementById('campComputeBox'); if(!box) return;
  var targets=sensibCampTargetCount();
  var groupSize=parseInt(document.getElementById('campGroupSize').value||'10')||10;
  var sessDur=parseFloat(document.getElementById('campSessionDur').value||'1')||1;
  var perDay=parseInt(document.getElementById('campSessionsPerDay').value||'2')||2;
  var nbSessions=targets>0?Math.ceil(targets/groupSize):0;
  var totalHours=nbSessions*sessDur;
  var nbDays=nbSessions>0?Math.ceil(nbSessions/perDay):0;
  var selDepts=Object.keys(_campSelDepts);
  var selSupers=Object.keys(_campSelSupers);
  var cards=[
    {label:'Personnes ciblées',val:targets,color:'var(--p4)',icon:'👥'},
    {label:'Sessions nécessaires',val:nbSessions,color:'var(--amber)',icon:'📋'},
    {label:'Durée totale',val:totalHours.toFixed(1)+'h',color:'var(--green)',icon:'⏱'},
    {label:'Jours estimés',val:nbDays,color:'var(--p3)',icon:'📆'},
    {label:'Départements',val:selDepts.length,color:'var(--text2)',icon:'🏭'},
    {label:'Superviseurs',val:selSupers.length,color:'var(--red)',icon:'🧑‍🏫'}
  ];
  box.innerHTML=cards.map(function(c){
    return '<div style="background:var(--bg3);border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:8px;padding:8px;text-align:center">'
      +'<div style="font-size:15px">'+c.icon+'</div>'
      +'<div style="font-size:18px;font-weight:700;color:'+c.color+'">'+c.val+'</div>'
      +'<div style="font-size:9px;color:var(--text3)">'+c.label+'</div></div>';
  }).join('');
}
function sensibCampMsg(txt,type){
  var el=document.getElementById('campMsg'); if(!el) return;
  el.textContent=txt;
  el.style.background=type==='ok'?'rgba(16,201,133,.1)':'rgba(232,68,90,.1)';
  el.style.color=type==='ok'?'var(--green)':'var(--red)';
  el.style.border='1px solid '+(type==='ok'?'rgba(16,201,133,.3)':'rgba(232,68,90,.3)');
  el.style.display='block';
  setTimeout(function(){ el.style.display='none'; },5000);
}
function sensibLaunchCampaign(){
  var obj=document.getElementById('campObjective').value.trim();
  var haz=document.getElementById('campHazard').value;
  var start=document.getElementById('campStart').value;
  var selDepts=Object.keys(_campSelDepts);
  if(!obj||!haz||!start){ sensibCampMsg('Renseignez l\'objectif, le type de risque et la date de début.','err'); return; }
  if(!selDepts.length){ sensibCampMsg('Sélectionnez au moins un département/poste ciblé.','err'); return; }
  var selSupers=Object.keys(_campSelSupers);
  var manual=document.getElementById('campManualSuper');
  if(manual&&manual.value.trim()) selSupers.push(manual.value.trim());
  var targets=sensibCampTargetCount();
  var groupSize=parseInt(document.getElementById('campGroupSize').value||'10')||10;
  var sessDur=parseFloat(document.getElementById('campSessionDur').value||'1')||1;
  var perDay=parseInt(document.getElementById('campSessionsPerDay').value||'2')||2;
  var nbSessions=targets>0?Math.ceil(targets/groupSize):0;
  var nbDays=nbSessions>0?Math.ceil(nbSessions/perDay):0;
  // Planning prévisionnel
  var planning=[]; var d=new Date(start); var remaining=nbSessions; var grp=1;
  while(remaining>0){
    var daySessions=Math.min(perDay,remaining);
    var dayPlan=[];
    for(var s=0;s<daySessions;s++){
      var sup=selSupers.length?selSupers[(grp-1)%selSupers.length]:'—';
      dayPlan.push({group:grp,supervisor:sup,size:Math.min(groupSize,targets-(grp-1)*groupSize)});
      grp++;
    }
    planning.push({date:d.toISOString().slice(0,10),sessions:dayPlan});
    remaining-=daySessions;
    d.setDate(d.getDate()+1);
  }
  var camp={
    id:Date.now(),
    objective:obj, hazard:haz, startDate:start,
    departments:selDepts, supervisors:selSupers,
    targetCount:targets, groupSize:groupSize, sessionDur:sessDur,
    nbSessions:nbSessions, nbDays:nbDays,
    planning:planning,
    status:'En cours', createdAt:new Date().toISOString()
  };
  _sensibCampaigns.unshift(camp);
  sensibSaveCampaigns();
  _campSelDepts={}; _campSelSupers={};
  document.getElementById('campObjective').value='';
  document.getElementById('campHazard').value='';
  document.getElementById('campStart').value='';
  sensibCampMsg('Campagne lancée avec succès !','ok');
  sensibToggleCampForm();
  sensibBuildCampaignUI();
}
// Avancement = sessions réalisées (depuis la date de début, risque + dept correspondants)
function sensibCampaignProgress(camp){
  var startMs=new Date(camp.startDate).getTime();
  var coveredMats={};
  _sensibData.forEach(function(r){
    if((r.dateMs||0)<startMs) return;
    if(camp.hazard && r.hazard!==camp.hazard) return;
    if(camp.departments.length && r.department && camp.departments.indexOf(r.department)<0) return;
    if(r.matricule) coveredMats[r.matricule]=1;
  });
  var covered=Object.keys(coveredMats).length;
  var coverage=camp.targetCount>0?Math.round(covered/camp.targetCount*100):0;
  var sessionsDone=0;
  _sensibData.forEach(function(r){
    if((r.dateMs||0)>=startMs && (!camp.hazard||r.hazard===camp.hazard) &&
       (!camp.departments.length||!r.department||camp.departments.indexOf(r.department)>=0)) sessionsDone++;
  });
  var realisation=camp.nbSessions>0?Math.round(Math.min(sessionsDone,camp.nbSessions)/camp.nbSessions*100):0;
  return {covered:covered,coverage:coverage,sessionsDone:sessionsDone,realisation:realisation};
}
function sensibCloseCampaign(id){
  var c=_sensibCampaigns.find(function(x){return x.id===id;});
  if(!c) return;
  var p=sensibCampaignProgress(c);
  c.status='Clôturée';
  c.results={covered:p.covered,coverage:p.coverage,sessionsDone:p.sessionsDone,realisation:p.realisation,closedAt:new Date().toISOString()};
  sensibSaveCampaigns();
  sensibBuildCampaignUI();
}
function sensibDeleteCampaign(id){
  _sensibCampaigns=_sensibCampaigns.filter(function(x){return x.id!==id;});
  sensibSaveCampaigns();
  sensibBuildCampaignUI();
}
function sensibTogglePlanning(id){
  var el=document.getElementById('campPlan_'+id);
  if(el) el.style.display=el.style.display==='none'?'block':'none';
}
function sensibBuildCampaignUI(){
  if(!_sensibCampaigns.length) sensibLoadCampaigns();
  var cont=document.getElementById('sensibCampList'); if(!cont) return;
  if(!_sensibCampaigns.length){
    cont.innerHTML='<div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text3);padding:8px 0">Aucune campagne active. Cliquez sur « Lancer une campagne » pour en créer une.</div>';
    return;
  }
  cont.innerHTML=_sensibCampaigns.map(function(c){
    var p=c.status==='Clôturée'&&c.results?c.results:sensibCampaignProgress(c);
    var statusCol=c.status==='Clôturée'?'var(--text3)':'var(--green)';
    var planRows=c.planning.map(function(d){
      return '<tr><td style="font-family:JetBrains Mono,monospace;font-size:10px;color:var(--text3)">'+escH(d.date)+'</td>'
        +'<td style="font-size:10px">'+d.sessions.map(function(s){return 'G'+s.group+' ('+s.size+'p · '+escH(s.supervisor)+')';}).join('<br>')+'</td></tr>';
    }).join('');
    var resultsBlock=c.status==='Clôturée'&&c.results?
      '<div style="margin-top:8px;padding:8px;background:rgba(16,201,133,.08);border:1px solid rgba(16,201,133,.25);border-radius:8px">'
      +'<div style="font-size:10px;font-weight:600;color:var(--green);margin-bottom:4px">✅ RÉSULTATS APRÈS CLÔTURE</div>'
      +'<div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text2)">Personnes couvertes : <strong>'+c.results.covered+'/'+c.targetCount+'</strong> · '
      +'Taux de couverture : <strong>'+c.results.coverage+'%</strong> · '
      +'Sessions réalisées : <strong>'+c.results.sessionsDone+'</strong> · '
      +'Taux de réalisation : <strong>'+c.results.realisation+'%</strong></div></div>':'';
    return '<div style="border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:10px;padding:12px;margin-bottom:10px;background:var(--bg2)">'
      +'<div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:flex-start;gap:8px;flex-wrap:wrap">'
        +'<div style="flex:1;min-width:200px">'
          +'<div style="font-size:13px;font-weight:700;color:var(--text)">🎯 '+escH(c.objective)+'</div>'
          +'<div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text3);margin-top:2px">⚠ '+escH(c.hazard)+' · 📅 début '+escH(c.startDate)+'</div>'
        +'</div>'
        +'<span style="font-size:10px;font-weight:600;padding:3px 10px;border-radius:14px;color:'+statusCol+';border:1px solid '+statusCol+'">'+escH(c.status)+'</span>'
      +'</div>'
      // Résumé
      +'<div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:repeat(auto-fill,minmax(120px,1fr));gap:8px;margin-top:10px">'
        +'<div><div style="font-size:9px;color:var(--text3)">Public cible</div><div style="font-size:11px;font-weight:600">'+c.departments.map(escH).join(', ')+'</div></div>'
        +'<div><div style="font-size:9px;color:var(--text3)">Auditeurs visés</div><div style="font-size:11px;font-weight:600;color:var(--p4)">'+c.targetCount+'</div></div>'
        +'<div><div style="font-size:9px;color:var(--text3)">Durée estimée</div><div style="font-size:11px;font-weight:600">'+(c.nbSessions*c.sessionDur).toFixed(1)+'h · '+c.nbDays+'j</div></div>'
        +'<div><div style="font-size:9px;color:var(--text3)">Superviseurs</div><div style="font-size:11px;font-weight:600">'+(c.supervisors.length?c.supervisors.map(escH).join(', '):'—')+'</div></div>'
      +'</div>'
      // Avancement
      +'<div style="margin-top:10px">'
        +'<div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;font-size:10px;color:var(--text2);margin-bottom:3px">'
          +'<span>Avancement (réalisation)</span><span style="color:var(--amber)">'+p.realisation+'% · '+p.sessionsDone+' session(s)</span></div>'
        +'<div style="background:var(--bg4);border-radius:4px;height:7px;overflow:hidden"><div style="height:100%;background:var(--amber);width:'+p.realisation+'%;border-radius:4px;transition:width .5s"></div></div>'
        +'<div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;font-size:10px;color:var(--text2);margin:6px 0 3px"><span>Taux de couverture</span><span style="color:var(--green)">'+p.coverage+'% · '+p.covered+'/'+c.targetCount+'</span></div>'
        +'<div style="background:var(--bg4);border-radius:4px;height:7px;overflow:hidden"><div style="height:100%;background:var(--green);width:'+p.coverage+'%;border-radius:4px;transition:width .5s"></div></div>'
      +'</div>'
      +resultsBlock
      // Actions
      +'<div style="display:flex;gap:8px;margin-top:10px;flex-wrap:wrap">'
        +'<button class="btn" style="font-size:10px;padding:3px 10px" onclick="sensibTogglePlanning('+c.id+')">📋 Planning prévisionnel</button>'
        +(c.status!=='Clôturée'?'<button class="btn" style="font-size:10px;padding:3px 10px;color:var(--green);border-color:rgba(16,201,133,.4)" onclick="sensibCloseCampaign('+c.id+')">✓ Clôturer</button>':'')
        +'<button class="btn" style="font-size:10px;padding:3px 10px;color:var(--red);border-color:rgba(232,68,90,.3)" onclick="sensibDeleteCampaign('+c.id+')">🗑 Supprimer</button>'
      +'</div>'
      // Planning (masqué)
      +'<div id="campPlan_'+c.id+'" style="display:none;margin-top:10px">'
        +'<div class="tblw"><table><thead><tr><th>Date</th><th>Sessions (groupe · taille · superviseur)</th></tr></thead><tbody>'+planRows+'</tbody></table></div>'
      +'</div>'
    +'</div>';
  }).join('');
}

function initSensib(d){
  _sensibData      = d.sensibilisation || [];
  _sensibEmployees = d.sensibilisationEmployees || [];
  _sensibTargets   = d.sensibilisationTargets || [];
  var srcLink=document.getElementById('sensibSourceLink');
  if(srcLink&&d.sensibilisationSourceUrl) srcLink.href=d.sensibilisationSourceUrl;
  var meta=document.getElementById('sensibSourceMeta');
  if(meta) meta.textContent=_sensibData.length+' session(s)';
  buildSensibFilters();
  buildSensibKpis();
  buildSensibProgressBars();
  buildSensibCharts();
  buildSensibLeaderboard();
  renderSensib();
}

// ── Brique 1 : KPIs ──────────────────────────────────────────
function buildSensibKpis(){
  var row=document.getElementById('sensibKpiRow'); if(!row) return;
  var total=_sensibData.length;
  var mats={};
  _sensibData.forEach(function(r){ if(r.matricule) mats[r.matricule]=1; });
  var covered=Object.keys(mats).length;
  var totalStaff=_sensibEmployees.length || covered;
  var coveragePct=totalStaff>0?Math.round(covered/totalStaff*100):0;
  var totalHours=0;
  _sensibData.forEach(function(r){ totalHours+=r.duration||0; });
  var hazards={};
  _sensibData.forEach(function(r){ if(r.hazard) hazards[r.hazard]=(hazards[r.hazard]||0)+1; });
  var kpis=[
    {label:'Sessions totales',    val:total,                      color:'var(--p4)',  icon:'🎓'},
    {label:'Employés touchés',    val:covered+'/'+totalStaff,      color:'var(--green)',icon:'👷'},
    {label:'Taux de couverture',  val:coveragePct+'%',            color:coveragePct>=80?'var(--green)':coveragePct>=50?'var(--amber)':'var(--red)', icon:'📊'},
    {label:'Heures investies',    val:totalHours.toFixed(1)+'h',  color:'var(--amber)',icon:'⏱'},
    {label:'Types de risque',     val:Object.keys(hazards).length, color:'var(--p3)',  icon:'⚠️'},
  ];
  row.innerHTML=kpis.map(function(k){
    return '<div class="kpi" style="flex:1;min-width:130px;display:flex;flex-direction:column;align-items:center;gap:2px">'
      +'<div style="font-size:18px">'+k.icon+'</div>'
      +'<div class="kpi-val" style="color:'+k.color+';font-size:22px">'+k.val+'</div>'
      +'<div class="kpi-lbl" style="text-align:center">'+k.label+'</div></div>';
  }).join('');
}

// ── Brique 1 : Progress bars Actual vs Target ──────────────────
function buildSensibProgressBars(){
  var cont=document.getElementById('sensibProgressBars'); if(!cont) return;
  var card=document.getElementById('sensibProgressCard');
  var hazards={};
  _sensibData.forEach(function(r){ if(r.hazard) hazards[r.hazard]=(hazards[r.hazard]||0)+1; });
  if(!_sensibTargets.length){
    if(card) card.style.display='none';
    return;
  }
  if(card) card.style.display='';
  cont.innerHTML=_sensibTargets.map(function(t){
    var actual=hazards[t.hazard]||0;
    var pct=t.target>0?Math.min(100,Math.round(actual/t.target*100)):0;
    var col=pct>=100?'var(--green)':pct>=60?'var(--amber)':'var(--red)';
    return '<div>'
      +'<div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;font-size:10px;color:var(--text2);margin-bottom:3px">'
      +'<span>'+escH(t.hazard)+'</span><span style="color:'+col+'">'+actual+' / '+t.target+' ('+pct+'%)</span></div>'
      +'<div style="background:var(--bg4);border-radius:4px;height:8px;overflow:hidden">'
      +'<div style="height:100%;border-radius:4px;background:'+col+';width:'+pct+'%;transition:width .6s ease"></div></div></div>';
  }).join('');
}

// ── Brique 1 : Graphiques ──────────────────────────────────────
var _SCOLS=['#0da8d2','#f5a623','#10c985','#e8445a','#7b5ea7','#4ab8c1','#d4a843','#6ec97b','#e88a5a'];
function buildSensibCharts(){
  function kill(k){ if(_sensibCharts[k]){ _sensibCharts[k].destroy(); delete _sensibCharts[k]; } }
  kill('hazard'); kill('dept'); kill('team');
  var hazards={}, depts={};
  _sensibData.forEach(function(r){
    if(r.hazard) hazards[r.hazard]=(hazards[r.hazard]||0)+1;
    if(r.department) depts[r.department]=(depts[r.department]||0)+1;
  });
  function mkBar(cid,labels,vals,key){
    var el=document.getElementById(cid); if(!el) return;
    _sensibCharts[key]=new Chart(el,{type:'bar',data:{labels:labels,datasets:[{data:vals,backgroundColor:_SCOLS.slice(0,vals.length),borderRadius:4}]},options:{responsive:true,maintainAspectRatio:false,plugins:{legend:{display:false}},scales:{x:{ticks:{color:'var(--text2)',font:{size:9}},grid:{display:false}},y:{ticks:{color:'var(--text3)',font:{size:9}},grid:{color:'rgba(255,255,255,.05)'}}}}});
  }
  var hK=Object.keys(hazards).sort(function(a,b){return hazards[b]-hazards[a];}).slice(0,8);
  mkBar('sensibHazardC',hK,hK.map(function(k){return hazards[k];}),'hazard');
  var dK=Object.keys(depts).sort(function(a,b){return depts[b]-depts[a];}).slice(0,8);
  mkBar('sensibDeptC',dK,dK.map(function(k){return depts[k];}),'dept');
}

// ── Brique 3 : Leaderboard formateurs ─────────────────────────
function buildSensibLeaderboard(){
  var lb=document.getElementById('sensibLeaderboard'); if(!lb) return;
  var trainers={};
  _sensibData.forEach(function(r){
    if(!r.trainer) return;
    if(!trainers[r.trainer]) trainers[r.trainer]={sessions:0,employees:{},hours:0};
    trainers[r.trainer].sessions++;
    if(r.matricule) trainers[r.trainer].employees[r.matricule]=1;
    trainers[r.trainer].hours+=r.duration||0;
  });
  var sorted=Object.keys(trainers).sort(function(a,b){return trainers[b].sessions-trainers[a].sessions;});
  if(!sorted.length){ lb.innerHTML='<div style="color:var(--text3);font-size:11px;padding:8px">Aucun formateur enregistré.</div>'; return; }
  var medals=['🥇','🥈','🥉'];
  lb.innerHTML=sorted.map(function(t,i){
    var tr=trainers[t];
    var empCount=Object.keys(tr.employees).length;
    return '<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:10px;padding:8px 10px;background:var(--bg3);border-radius:8px;border:1px solid var(--border)">'
      +'<div style="font-size:18px;flex-shrink:0">'+(medals[i]||'#'+(i+1))+'</div>'
      +'<div style="flex:1;min-width:0"><div style="font-weight:600;font-size:12px;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;white-space:nowrap">'+escH(t)+'</div>'
      +'<div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text3)">'+tr.sessions+' sessions · '+empCount+' employés · '+tr.hours.toFixed(1)+'h</div></div>'
      +'<div style="font-size:12px;font-weight:700;color:var(--amber)">'+tr.sessions+'</div></div>';
  }).join('');

  // Team comparison chart
  function kill(k){ if(_sensibCharts[k]){ _sensibCharts[k].destroy(); delete _sensibCharts[k]; } }
  kill('team');
  var el=document.getElementById('sensibTeamC'); if(!el) return;
  var labels=sorted.slice(0,6).map(function(t){return t.split(' ')[0];});
  var ds1=sorted.slice(0,6).map(function(t){return trainers[t].sessions;});
  var ds2=sorted.slice(0,6).map(function(t){return Object.keys(trainers[t].employees).length;});
  var ds3=sorted.slice(0,6).map(function(t){return +trainers[t].hours.toFixed(1);});
  _sensibCharts['team']=new Chart(el,{type:'bar',data:{labels:labels,datasets:[
    {label:'Sessions',data:ds1,backgroundColor:'rgba(13,168,210,.7)',borderRadius:3},
    {label:'Employés',data:ds2,backgroundColor:'rgba(245,166,35,.7)',borderRadius:3},
    {label:'Heures',data:ds3,backgroundColor:'rgba(16,201,133,.7)',borderRadius:3}
  ]},options:{responsive:true,maintainAspectRatio:false,plugins:{legend:{labels:{color:'var(--text2)',font:{size:9}}}},scales:{x:{ticks:{color:'var(--text2)',font:{size:9}},grid:{display:false}},y:{ticks:{color:'var(--text3)',font:{size:9}},grid:{color:'rgba(255,255,255,.05)'}}}}});
}

// ── Brique 2 : Recherche individuelle ─────────────────────────
function sensibSearchEmployee(){
  var q=document.getElementById('sensibEmpSearch').value.trim().toLowerCase();
  var res=document.getElementById('sensibEmpResults');
  var profile=document.getElementById('sensibEmpProfile');
  var empty=document.getElementById('sensibEmpEmpty');
  if(!q){ res.style.display='none'; profile.style.display='none'; empty.style.display=''; _sensibSelectedMat=null; return; }
  // Search in employees list + session data
  var found={};
  _sensibEmployees.forEach(function(e){
    if((e.name||'').toLowerCase().indexOf(q)>-1||(e.matricule||'').indexOf(q)>-1) found[e.matricule]=e;
  });
  _sensibData.forEach(function(r){
    if(!found[r.matricule]&&((r.name||'').toLowerCase().indexOf(q)>-1||(r.matricule||'').indexOf(q)>-1)){
      found[r.matricule]={matricule:r.matricule,name:r.name,department:r.department};
    }
  });
  var list=Object.values(found).slice(0,10);
  if(!list.length){ res.innerHTML='<div style="padding:8px 12px;font-size:11px;color:var(--text3)">Aucun employé trouvé</div>'; res.style.display='block'; profile.style.display='none'; empty.style.display='none'; return; }
  res.innerHTML=list.map(function(e){
    return '<div style="padding:8px 12px;cursor:pointer;font-size:11px;border-bottom:1px solid var(--border);transition:background .15s" '
      +'onmouseover="this.style.background=\'var(--bg4)\'" onmouseout="this.style.background=\'\'" '
      +'onclick="sensibSelectEmployee(\''+escH(e.matricule)+'\')">'
      +'<strong>'+escH(e.name||e.matricule)+'</strong> <span style="color:var(--text3)">— '+escH(e.matricule)+(e.department?' · '+escH(e.department):'')+'</span></div>';
  }).join('');
  res.style.display='block'; profile.style.display='none'; empty.style.display='none';
}

function sensibSelectEmployee(mat){
  _sensibSelectedMat=mat;
  document.getElementById('sensibEmpResults').style.display='none';
  // Find employee info
  var emp=_sensibEmployees.find(function(e){return e.matricule===mat;});
  if(!emp) {
    var firstSess=_sensibData.find(function(r){return r.matricule===mat;});
    if(firstSess) emp={matricule:mat,name:firstSess.name,department:firstSess.department};
    else emp={matricule:mat,name:'—',department:'—'};
  }
  // Filter sessions for this employee
  var history=_sensibData.filter(function(r){return r.matricule===mat;}).sort(function(a,b){return (b.dateMs||0)-(a.dateMs||0);});
  var lastSession=history.length?history[0].timestamp:'—';
  // Profile card
  var card=document.getElementById('sensibEmpProfileCard');
  card.innerHTML=[
    {label:'Nom',val:emp.name||mat},
    {label:'Matricule',val:mat},
    {label:'Département',val:emp.department||'—'},
    {label:'Sessions assistées',val:history.length},
    {label:'Dernière sensibilisation',val:lastSession}
  ].map(function(f){
    return '<div style="min-width:130px"><div style="font-size:9px;color:var(--text3);margin-bottom:2px">'+f.label+'</div>'
      +'<div style="font-size:12px;font-weight:600;color:var(--text)">'+escH(String(f.val))+'</div></div>';
  }).join('');
  // Gap Alert: check if any session in last 6 months for mandatory hazards by dept
  var gapDiv=document.getElementById('sensibGapAlert');
  var sixMonthsAgo=Date.now()-6*30*24*3600*1000;
  var dept=(emp.department||'').toLowerCase();
  var mandatoryHazards=[];
  if(dept.indexOf('cuisson')>-1||dept.indexOf('baking')>-1) mandatoryHazards=['Brûlure','Risque mécanique','Incendie / Explosion'];
  else if(dept.indexOf('emballage')>-1||dept.indexOf('packaging')>-1) mandatoryHazards=['Risque mécanique','Hygiène / Sécurité alimentaire'];
  else if(dept.indexOf('production')>-1) mandatoryHazards=['Glissade / Chute','Risque mécanique'];
  var gaps=mandatoryHazards.filter(function(h){
    return !history.some(function(s){ return s.hazard===h && (s.dateMs||0)>sixMonthsAgo; });
  });
  if(gaps.length){
    gapDiv.innerHTML='⚠️ <strong>GAP ALERT</strong> — Sensibilisation(s) obligatoire(s) manquante(s) ces 6 derniers mois pour ce poste : <strong>'+gaps.map(escH).join(', ')+'</strong>';
    gapDiv.style.display='block';
  } else { gapDiv.style.display='none'; }
  // History table
  var tb=document.getElementById('sensibEmpHistoryBody');
  if(!history.length){
    tb.innerHTML='<tr><td colspan="6" style="text-align:center;color:var(--text3);padding:16px">Aucune session enregistrée</td></tr>';
  } else {
    tb.innerHTML=history.map(function(r){
      var statusCol=r.status==='Absent'?'var(--red)':'var(--green)';
      var linkCell=sensibPjButton(r.attendanceUrl);
      return '<tr>'
        +'<td style="font-size:10px;font-family:JetBrains Mono,monospace;color:var(--text3)">'+escH(r.timestamp)+'</td>'
        +'<td style="font-size:11px">'+escH(r.theme||'—')+'</td>'
        +'<td><span class="rbadge" style="background:rgba(245,166,35,.15);color:var(--amber);border:1px solid rgba(245,166,35,.3)">'+escH(r.hazard||'—')+'</span></td>'
        +'<td style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text2)">'+escH(r.trainer||'—')+'</td>'
        +'<td style="color:'+statusCol+';font-size:10px;font-weight:600">'+escH(r.status||'Présent')+'</td>'
        +'<td style="text-align:center">'+linkCell+'</td>'
        +'</tr>';
    }).join('');
  }
  document.getElementById('sensibEmpProfile').style.display='block';
  document.getElementById('sensibEmpEmpty').style.display='none';
}

// ── Pièce jointe : bouton + viewer intégré (aucune ouverture externe) ──
// Extrait l'ID Drive de n'importe quel format de lien.
function sensibDriveFileId(url){
  if(!url) return '';
  var m=String(url).match(/\/file\/d\/([a-zA-Z0-9_-]+)/)
      ||String(url).match(/[?&]id=([a-zA-Z0-9_-]+)/)
      ||String(url).match(/\/d\/([a-zA-Z0-9_-]+)/);
  return m?m[1]:'';
}
function sensibPjButton(url){
  var id=sensibDriveFileId(url);
  if(!id) return '<span style="color:var(--text3);font-size:10px">—</span>';
  return '<button onclick="sensibViewPj(\''+id+'\')" '
    +'style="background:rgba(74,144,226,.15);color:var(--p4);border:1px solid rgba(74,144,226,.35);'
    +'border-radius:6px;padding:3px 9px;font-size:11px;cursor:pointer;font-weight:600" '
    +'title="Afficher la pièce jointe dans le dashboard">📋 Voir PJ</button>';
}
function sensibViewPj(id){
  var ov=document.getElementById('sensibPjModal');
  var fr=document.getElementById('sensibPjFrame');
  // /preview = viewer intégré Google Drive (iframe), pas de redirection externe.
  fr.src='https://drive.google.com/file/d/'+id+'/preview';
  ov.style.display='flex';
}
function sensibClosePj(){
  var ov=document.getElementById('sensibPjModal');
  document.getElementById('sensibPjFrame').src='';
  ov.style.display='none';
}

function sensibClearEmployee(){
  _sensibSelectedMat=null;
  document.getElementById('sensibEmpSearch').value='';
  document.getElementById('sensibEmpResults').style.display='none';
  document.getElementById('sensibEmpProfile').style.display='none';
  document.getElementById('sensibEmpEmpty').style.display='';
}

// ── Filtres registre général ───────────────────────────────────
function buildSensibFilters(){
  var hazards={},depts={},trainers={};
  _sensibData.forEach(function(r){
    if(r.hazard) hazards[r.hazard]=1;
    if(r.department) depts[r.department]=1;
    if(r.trainer) trainers[r.trainer]=1;
  });
  function fillSel(id,obj){
    var sel=document.getElementById(id); if(!sel) return;
    var cur=sel.value;
    sel.innerHTML='<option value="all">Tous</option>';
    Object.keys(obj).sort().forEach(function(k){ var o=document.createElement('option'); o.value=k; o.textContent=k; sel.appendChild(o); });
    if(cur&&obj[cur]) sel.value=cur;
  }
  fillSel('sensibFilterHazard',hazards);
  fillSel('sensibFilterDept',depts);
  fillSel('sensibFilterTrainer',trainers);
}

function renderSensib(){
  var q=(document.getElementById('sensibSearch')||{}).value||'';
  var fh=(document.getElementById('sensibFilterHazard')||{}).value||'all';
  var fd=(document.getElementById('sensibFilterDept')||{}).value||'all';
  var ft=(document.getElementById('sensibFilterTrainer')||{}).value||'all';
  var sort=(document.getElementById('sensibSort')||{}).value||'date_desc';
  var rows=_sensibData.filter(function(r){
    if(fh!=='all'&&r.hazard!==fh) return false;
    if(fd!=='all'&&r.department!==fd) return false;
    if(ft!=='all'&&r.trainer!==ft) return false;
    if(q){ var lq=q.toLowerCase(); var s=(r.name+' '+r.department+' '+r.hazard+' '+r.trainer+' '+r.matricule+' '+r.theme).toLowerCase(); if(s.indexOf(lq)<0) return false; }
    return true;
  });
  rows.sort(function(a,b){
    if(sort==='date_desc') return (b.dateMs||0)-(a.dateMs||0);
    if(sort==='date_asc')  return (a.dateMs||0)-(b.dateMs||0);
    if(sort==='name_az')   return (a.name||'').localeCompare(b.name||'');
    if(sort==='dept_az')   return (a.department||'').localeCompare(b.department||'');
    if(sort==='hazard_az') return (a.hazard||'').localeCompare(b.hazard||'');
    return 0;
  });
  var cnt=document.getElementById('sensibListCount'); if(cnt) cnt.textContent=rows.length+' / '+_sensibData.length;
  var tb=document.getElementById('sensibBody'); if(!tb) return;
  if(!rows.length){ tb.innerHTML='<tr><td colspan="10" style="text-align:center;color:var(--text3);padding:20px">Aucune session trouvée</td></tr>'; return; }
  tb.innerHTML=rows.map(function(r){
    var statusCol=r.status==='Absent'?'var(--red)':'var(--green)';
    var linkCell=sensibPjButton(r.attendanceUrl);
    return '<tr>'
      +'<td style="font-family:JetBrains Mono,monospace;font-size:10px;color:var(--text3)">'+escH(r.timestamp)+'</td>'
      +'<td style="font-family:JetBrains Mono,monospace;font-size:11px">'+escH(r.matricule)+'</td>'
      +'<td style="font-weight:500">'+escH(r.name)+'</td>'
      +'<td style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text2)">'+escH(r.department)+'</td>'
      +'<td><span class="rbadge" style="background:rgba(245,166,35,.15);color:var(--amber);border:1px solid rgba(245,166,35,.3)">'+escH(r.hazard||'—')+'</span></td>'
      +'<td style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text2)">'+escH(r.theme||'—')+'</td>'
      +'<td style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text2)">'+escH(r.trainer)+'</td>'
      +'<td style="font-size:11px;text-align:center">'+((r.duration||0)>0?r.duration+'h':'—')+'</td>'
      +'<td style="color:'+statusCol+';font-size:10px;font-weight:600">'+escH(r.status||'Présent')+'</td>'
      +'<td style="text-align:center">'+linkCell+'</td>'
      +'</tr>';
  }).join('');
}

function clearSensibFilters(){
  ['sensibSearch','sensibFilterHazard','sensibFilterDept','sensibFilterTrainer'].forEach(function(id){
    var el=document.getElementById(id); if(el){if(el.tagName==='INPUT')el.value='';else el.value=el.options[0].value;}
  });
  renderSensib();
}

// ── Brique 4 : Autocomplete matricule ─────────────────────────
function sensibGetEmpList(){
  var all={};
  _sensibEmployees.forEach(function(e){ if(e.matricule) all[e.matricule]=e; });
  _sensibData.forEach(function(r){ if(r.matricule&&!all[r.matricule]) all[r.matricule]={matricule:r.matricule,name:r.name,department:r.department}; });
  return Object.values(all);
}
function sensibMatInput(){
  var q=(document.getElementById('sensibFormMat').value||'').trim().toLowerCase();
  var sug=document.getElementById('sensibMatSuggest');
  if(!q){sug.style.display='none';return;}
  var list=sensibGetEmpList().filter(function(e){
    return (e.matricule||'').toLowerCase().indexOf(q)>-1||(e.name||'').toLowerCase().indexOf(q)>-1;
  }).slice(0,10);
  if(!list.length){sug.style.display='none';return;}
  sug.innerHTML=list.map(function(e,i){
    return '<div data-idx="'+i+'" style="padding:7px 12px;cursor:pointer;font-size:11px;border-bottom:1px solid var(--border);transition:background .12s" '
      +'onmousedown="sensibPickEmployee(\''+escH(e.matricule)+'\',\''+escH(e.name)+'\',\''+escH(e.department||'')+'\');event.preventDefault()" '
      +'onmouseover="this.style.background=\'var(--bg4)\'" onmouseout="this.style.background=\'\'">'
      +'<strong style="color:var(--p4)">'+escH(e.matricule)+'</strong>'
      +' — '+escH(e.name||'—')
      +(e.department?'<span style="color:var(--text3);font-size:10px"> · '+escH(e.department)+'</span>':'')
      +'</div>';
  }).join('');
  sug.style.display='block';
}
function sensibMatKey(e){
  if(e.key==='Escape'||e.key==='Tab') document.getElementById('sensibMatSuggest').style.display='none';
}
function sensibPickEmployee(mat,name,dept){
  document.getElementById('sensibFormMat').value=mat;
  document.getElementById('sensibFormName').value=name;
  document.getElementById('sensibFormDept').value=dept;
  document.getElementById('sensibMatSuggest').style.display='none';
}

// ── Brique 4 : Gestion multi-participants ──────────────────────
function sensibAddParticipant(){
  var mat=(document.getElementById('sensibFormMat').value||'').trim();
  var name=(document.getElementById('sensibFormName').value||'').trim();
  var dept=(document.getElementById('sensibFormDept').value||'').trim();
  if(!mat||!name){sensibShowMsg('Matricule et Nom obligatoires pour ajouter un participant.','err');return;}
  if(_sensibParticipants.some(function(p){return p.matricule===mat;})){
    sensibShowMsg('Ce participant est déjà dans la liste.','err'); return;
  }
  _sensibParticipants.push({matricule:mat,name:name,department:dept});
  document.getElementById('sensibFormMat').value='';
  document.getElementById('sensibFormName').value='';
  document.getElementById('sensibFormDept').value='';
  document.getElementById('sensibMatSuggest').style.display='none';
  sensibRenderParticipants();
}
function sensibRemoveParticipant(mat){
  _sensibParticipants=_sensibParticipants.filter(function(p){return p.matricule!==mat;});
  sensibRenderParticipants();
}
function sensibRenderParticipants(){
  var panel=document.getElementById('sensibParticipantsPanel');
  var empty=document.getElementById('sensibParticipantsEmpty');
  var cnt=document.getElementById('sensibParticipantCount');
  var list=document.getElementById('sensibParticipantsList');
  if(!_sensibParticipants.length){
    panel.style.display='none'; empty.style.display=''; return;
  }
  panel.style.display=''; empty.style.display='none';
  cnt.textContent=_sensibParticipants.length;
  list.innerHTML=_sensibParticipants.map(function(p){
    return '<div style="display:inline-flex;align-items:center;gap:6px;padding:4px 10px;background:var(--bg4);'
      +'border-radius:20px;border:1px solid var(--border);font-size:11px">'
      +'<span style="color:var(--p4);font-weight:600">'+escH(p.matricule)+'</span>'
      +'<span>'+escH(p.name)+'</span>'
      +(p.department?'<span style="color:var(--text3);font-size:9px">'+escH(p.department)+'</span>':'')
      +'<button onclick="sensibRemoveParticipant(\''+escH(p.matricule)+'\')" style="background:none;border:none;color:var(--red);cursor:pointer;font-size:12px;padding:0 2px;line-height:1">✕</button>'
      +'</div>';
  }).join('');
}

// ── Brique 4 : Upload & formulaire ────────────────────────────
function sensibHandleFile(input){
  var file=input.files[0]; if(!file) return;
  _sensibFile=file;
  var prev=document.getElementById('sensibFilePreview');
  prev.innerHTML='📎 '+escH(file.name)+' ('+Math.round(file.size/1024)+' Ko)';
  prev.style.display='block';
  document.getElementById('sensibDropZone').style.borderColor='var(--green)';
}
function sensibHandleDrop(e){
  e.preventDefault();
  document.getElementById('sensibDropZone').style.borderColor='var(--border)';
  var file=e.dataTransfer.files[0]; if(!file) return;
  _sensibFile=file;
  var prev=document.getElementById('sensibFilePreview');
  prev.innerHTML='📎 '+escH(file.name)+' ('+Math.round(file.size/1024)+' Ko)';
  prev.style.display='block';
}
function sensibShowMsg(txt,type){
  var el=document.getElementById('sensibFormMsg');
  if(!el) return;
  el.textContent=txt;
  el.style.background=type==='ok'?'rgba(16,201,133,.1)':'rgba(232,68,90,.1)';
  el.style.color=type==='ok'?'var(--green)':'var(--red)';
  el.style.border='1px solid '+(type==='ok'?'rgba(16,201,133,.3)':'rgba(232,68,90,.3)');
  el.style.display='block';
  setTimeout(function(){ el.style.display='none'; }, 5000);
}
function sensibSubmitForm(){
  var hazard=document.getElementById('sensibFormHazard').value;
  var trainer=document.getElementById('sensibFormTrainer').value.trim();
  var dateVal=document.getElementById('sensibFormDate').value;
  if(!hazard||!trainer||!dateVal){ sensibShowMsg('Veuillez remplir les champs obligatoires : date, type de risque et formateur.','err'); return; }
  if(!_sensibParticipants.length){ sensibShowMsg('Ajoutez au moins un participant avant d\'enregistrer.','err'); return; }
  if(!_sensibFile){ sensibShowMsg('⚠️ La feuille d\'émargement (photo / PDF) est obligatoire.','err'); return; }
  var btn=document.getElementById('sensibSubmitBtn');
  btn.disabled=true; btn.textContent='Enregistrement…';
  var commonData={
    hazard:hazard,
    trainer:trainer,
    theme:document.getElementById('sensibFormTheme').value.trim(),
    duration:parseFloat(document.getElementById('sensibFormDur').value||'0')||0,
    status:document.getElementById('sensibFormStatus').value
  };
  function saveAllParticipants(attendanceUrl){
    var participants=_sensibParticipants.slice();
    var saved=0,errors=0;
    function saveNext(){
      if(!participants.length){
        btn.disabled=false; btn.textContent='✅ Enregistrer la session';
        if(errors===0) sensibShowMsg(saved+' participant(s) enregistré(s) avec succès !','ok');
        else sensibShowMsg(saved+' enregistré(s), '+errors+' erreur(s).','err');
        if(errors===0) sensibResetForm();
        return;
      }
      var p=participants.shift();
      var data=Object.assign({},commonData,{matricule:p.matricule,name:p.name,department:p.department,attendanceUrl:attendanceUrl||''});
      google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(r){
        if(r&&r.success) saved++; else errors++;
        saveNext();
      }).withFailureHandler(function(){ errors++; saveNext(); }).addSensibilisationRecord(data);
    }
    saveNext();
  }
  // PJ obligatoire — upload bloquant
  var reader=new FileReader();
  reader.onload=function(ev){
    var b64=ev.target.result.split(',')[1];
    var riskType=(hazard||'risque').replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9]/g,'_');
    btn.textContent='⬆️ Upload Drive…';
    google.script.run
      .withSuccessHandler(function(r){
        if(!r||!r.success||!r.url){
          btn.disabled=false; btn.textContent='✅ Enregistrer la session';
          sensibShowMsg('❌ Échec upload Drive : '+(r&&r.error?r.error:'réponse vide'),'err');
          return;
        }
        // Indicateur : upload OK
        var prev=document.getElementById('sensibFilePreview');
        if(prev) prev.innerHTML='✅ Fichier uploadé — <span style="color:var(--green);font-size:10px">lien Drive généré</span>';
        saveAllParticipants(r.url);
      })
      .withFailureHandler(function(e){
        btn.disabled=false; btn.textContent='✅ Enregistrer la session';
        sensibShowMsg('❌ Erreur réseau lors de l\'upload Drive : '+(e&&e.message?e.message:e),'err');
      })
      .uploadAttendanceToSensibDrive(b64,_sensibFile.type,dateVal,riskType);
  };
  reader.readAsDataURL(_sensibFile);
}
function sensibResetForm(){
  ['sensibFormMat','sensibFormName','sensibFormDept','sensibFormTheme','sensibFormTrainer','sensibFormDur','sensibFormDate'].forEach(function(id){
    var el=document.getElementById(id); if(el) el.value='';
  });
  var hz=document.getElementById('sensibFormHazard'); if(hz) hz.value='';
  var st=document.getElementById('sensibFormStatus'); if(st) st.value='Présent';
  _sensibFile=null; _sensibParticipants=[];
  var prev=document.getElementById('sensibFilePreview'); if(prev) prev.style.display='none';
  var dz=document.getElementById('sensibDropZone'); if(dz) dz.style.borderColor='var(--border)';
  var fi=document.getElementById('sensibFileInput'); if(fi) fi.value='';
  sensibRenderParticipants();
}
function escH(s){return String(s||'').replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;').replace(/"/g,'&quot;');}

// ══ PRODUITS CHIMIQUES ET FDS ══════════════════════════════════
var _chimiquesData = [];

function chimiquesLoadOnDemand() {
  if (_chimiquesData.length) { chimiquesRender(); return; }
  var meta = document.getElementById('chimiquesSourceMeta');
  if (meta) meta.textContent = '⏳ Chargement…';
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(r) {
      _chimiquesData = r && r.items ? r.items : [];
      if (meta) meta.textContent = 'Source : Liste produits chimiques et FDS · '
        + _chimiquesData.filter(function(x){return !x.isCategory;}).length + ' produits';
      chimiquesPopulateFilters();
      chimiquesRender();
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(e) {
      if (meta) meta.textContent = '❌ Erreur : ' + (e && e.message ? e.message : e);
    })
    .getChimiquesForClient();
}

function chimiquesPopulateFilters() {
  var emps = {};
  _chimiquesData.forEach(function(r) { if (!r.isCategory && r.emplacement) emps[r.emplacement] = 1; });
  var sel = document.getElementById('chimiquesFilterEmp');
  if (!sel) return;
  var cur = sel.value;
  while (sel.options.length > 1) sel.remove(1);
  Object.keys(emps).sort().forEach(function(e) {
    var o = document.createElement('option'); o.value = e; o.textContent = e; sel.appendChild(o);
  });
  sel.value = cur;
}

function chimiquesResetFilters() {
  ['chimiquesSearch','chimiquesFilterFds','chimiquesFilterEmp'].forEach(function(id){
    var el = document.getElementById(id); if (!el) return;
    if (el.tagName === 'INPUT') el.value = ''; else el.value = el.options[0].value;
  });
  chimiquesRender();
}

function chimiquesRender() {
  var search = (document.getElementById('chimiquesSearch') || {}).value || '';
  var fdsF   = (document.getElementById('chimiquesFilterFds') || {}).value || '';
  var empF   = (document.getElementById('chimiquesFilterEmp') || {}).value || '';
  search = search.toLowerCase();
  var total = 0, fdsOk = 0, fdsMissing = 0;
  _chimiquesData.forEach(function(r) {
    if (r.isCategory) return;
    total++;
    if (r.fds.toLowerCase() === 'oui') fdsOk++;
    else fdsMissing++;
  });
  var kpiRow = document.getElementById('chimiquesKpiRow');
  if (kpiRow) {
    var pct = total > 0 ? Math.round(fdsOk / total * 100) : 0;
    kpiRow.innerHTML = [
      {label:'Total produits', val:total, color:'var(--p4)'},
      {label:'FDS disponibles', val:fdsOk, color:'var(--green)'},
      {label:'FDS manquantes', val:fdsMissing, color:'var(--red)'},
      {label:'Taux FDS', val:pct+'%', color:pct>=80?'var(--green)':pct>=50?'var(--amber)':'var(--red)'}
    ].map(function(k){
      return '<div style="flex:1;min-width:120px;background:var(--bg3);border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:10px;padding:12px 16px;text-align:center">'
        +'<div style="font-size:20px;font-weight:700;color:'+k.color+'">'+k.val+'</div>'
        +'<div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text3);margin-top:2px">'+k.label+'</div>'
        +'</div>';
    }).join('');
  }
  var rows = _chimiquesData.filter(function(r) {
    if (r.isCategory) return true;
    if (fdsF && r.fds.toLowerCase() !== fdsF) return false;
    if (empF && r.emplacement !== empF) return false;
    if (search) {
      var hay = (r.name+' '+r.emplacement+' '+r.localisation).toLowerCase();
      if (hay.indexOf(search) === -1) return false;
    }
    return true;
  });
  var dataRows = rows.filter(function(r){return !r.isCategory;});
  var cnt = document.getElementById('chimiquesCount');
  if (cnt) cnt.textContent = dataRows.length + ' / ' + total;
  var tb = document.getElementById('chimiquesBody');
  if (!tb) return;
  if (!dataRows.length) {
    tb.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="5" style="text-align:center;color:var(--text3);padding:20px">Aucun produit trouvé</td></tr>';
    return;
  }
  var html = '';
  rows.forEach(function(r) {
    if (r.isCategory) {
      html += '<tr style="background:rgba(245,166,35,.12)">'
        +'<td colspan="5" style="font-weight:700;color:var(--amber);font-size:12px;padding:8px 12px;letter-spacing:.5px">▶ '+escH(r.name)+'</td>'
        +'</tr>';
      return;
    }
    var fdsCell;
    if (r.fds.toLowerCase() === 'oui') {
      if (r.fdsUrl) {
        fdsCell = '<button onclick="chimiquesViewFds(\''+escH(r.fdsUrl)+'\')" '
          +'style="background:rgba(16,201,133,.15);color:var(--green);border:1px solid rgba(16,201,133,.3);'
          +'border-radius:6px;padding:3px 9px;font-size:11px;cursor:pointer;font-weight:600">📄 Voir FDS</button>';
      } else {
        fdsCell = '<span style="color:var(--green);font-size:11px;font-weight:600">✅ Oui</span>';
      }
    } else if (r.fds.toLowerCase() === 'non' || !r.fds) {
      fdsCell = '<span style="color:var(--red);font-size:11px;font-weight:600">❌ Manquante</span>';
    } else {
      fdsCell = '<span style="color:var(--text2);font-size:11px">'+escH(r.fds)+'</span>';
    }
    html += '<tr>'
      +'<td style="font-weight:500">'+escH(r.name)+'</td>'
      +'<td style="text-align:center;font-family:\'JetBrains Mono\',monospace;font-size:11px">'+escH(r.qty||'—')+'</td>'
      +'<td style="text-align:center">'+fdsCell+'</td>'
      +'<td style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text2)">'+escH(r.emplacement||'—')+'</td>'
      +'<td style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text3)">'+escH(r.localisation||'—')+'</td>'
      +'</tr>';
  });
  tb.innerHTML = html;
}

function chimiquesViewFds(url) {
  var id = sensibDriveFileId(url);
  if (id) {
    sensibViewPj(id);
  } else {
    var ov = document.getElementById('sensibPjModal');
    var fr = document.getElementById('sensibPjFrame');
    if (ov && fr) { fr.src = url; ov.style.display = 'flex'; }
  }
}

// ══ NAVIGATION ════════════════════════════════════════════════
function goTab(id,el){
  document.querySelectorAll('.page').forEach(function(p){p.classList.remove('on');});
  document.querySelectorAll('.tab').forEach(function(t){t.classList.remove('on');});
  document.getElementById(id).classList.add('on'); el.classList.add('on');
}
function goAI(){
  document.querySelectorAll('.tab').forEach(function(t){t.classList.remove('on');});
  document.querySelectorAll('.page').forEach(function(p){p.classList.remove('on');});
  document.getElementById('ai').classList.add('on');
}
function goVeille(){
  document.querySelectorAll('.tab').forEach(function(t){
    t.classList.toggle('on', /goTab\('veille'/.test(t.getAttribute('onclick')||''));
  });
  document.querySelectorAll('.page').forEach(function(p){p.classList.remove('on');});
  document.getElementById('veille').classList.add('on');
}

// ══ MODALS ════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function openModal(id){ document.getElementById(id).style.display='flex'; document.body.style.overflow='hidden'; }
function closeModal(id){ document.getElementById(id).style.display='none'; document.body.style.overflow=''; }
document.addEventListener('keydown',function(e){
  if(e.key==='Escape') ['incModal','accModal','tagModal','cleanModal','clnPlanModal','clnProductsModal','clnEmbedModal','permitDetailModal'].forEach(function(id){closeModal(id);});
});
function switchTab(prefix,tab,el){
  var panel=el.closest('.modal-panel');
  panel.querySelectorAll('[id^="'+prefix+'-"]').forEach(function(d){d.style.display='none';});
  panel.querySelectorAll('.modal-tab').forEach(function(t){t.classList.remove('on');});
  document.getElementById(prefix+'-'+tab).style.display='block'; el.classList.add('on');
}

// ══ NOTIFICATIONS ════════════════════════════════════════════
function buildNotifications(){
  if(!D||!D.planning) return;
  var todayItems=[], tomorrowItems=[], fumigWarn=[];
  D.planning.forEach(function(p){
    if(!p.isoDate) return;
    var isFumig=p.fumigation||p.activite.toLowerCase().indexOf('fumig')>-1;
    if(p.isoDate===TODAY_ISO) todayItems.push(p);
    else if(p.isoDate===TOMORROW_ISO) tomorrowItems.push(p);
    if(isFumig&&p.isoDate>TODAY_ISO){
      var j=diffDays(p.isoDate,TODAY_ISO);
      if(j>=1&&j<=6) fumigWarn.push({p:p,jours:j});
    }
  });
  var totalNormal=todayItems.length+tomorrowItems.length;
  var badge=document.getElementById('notifBadge');
  if(totalNormal>0){badge.textContent=totalNormal>9?'9+':String(totalNormal);badge.classList.add('show');}
  else badge.classList.remove('show');
  var badgeFum=document.getElementById('notifBadgeFum');
  if(fumigWarn.length>0) badgeFum.classList.add('show'); else badgeFum.classList.remove('show');
  var total=totalNormal+fumigWarn.length;
  document.getElementById('notifCount').textContent=total+' événement'+(total>1?'s':'');
  var list=document.getElementById('notifList');
  if(total===0){
    list.innerHTML='<div class="notif-empty">✅ Aucun événement aujourd\'hui ni demain</div>';
  } else {
    var html='';
    fumigWarn.forEach(function(fw){
      html+='<div class="notif-item fumig-warn"><span class="notif-lbl lbl-fumig">🦟 FUMIGATION J-'+fw.jours+'</span>'
        +'<div class="notif-act">'+esc(fw.p.activite)+'</div>'
        +'<div class="notif-det">'+esc(fw.p.details)+'</div>'
        +'<div class="notif-date">📅 '+fw.p.date+'</div></div>';
    });
    todayItems.forEach(function(p){
      html+='<div class="notif-item today"><span class="notif-lbl lbl-today">📅 Aujourd\'hui</span>'
        +'<div class="notif-act">'+esc(p.activite)+(p.fumigation?' 🦟':'')+'</div>'
        +'<div class="notif-det">'+esc(p.details)+'</div>'
        +'<div class="notif-date">'+p.date+'</div></div>';
    });
    tomorrowItems.forEach(function(p){
      html+='<div class="notif-item tomorrow"><span class="notif-lbl lbl-tomorrow">📅 Demain</span>'
        +'<div class="notif-act">'+esc(p.activite)+(p.fumigation?' 🦟':'')+'</div>'
        +'<div class="notif-det">'+esc(p.details)+'</div>'
        +'<div class="notif-date">'+p.date+'</div></div>';
    });
    list.innerHTML=html;
  }
  // Alerte fumigation Vue Globale
  var alert=document.getElementById('fumigAlert');
  var fumigToday=todayItems.filter(function(p){return p.fumigation;});
  if(fumigToday.length>0){
    alert.classList.add('show');
    document.getElementById('fumigTitle').textContent='🦟 FUMIGATION AUJOURD\'HUI';
    document.getElementById('fumigSub').innerHTML='<strong>'+esc(fumigToday[0].activite)+'</strong> — Préparez toutes les zones.';
  } else if(fumigWarn.length>0){
    fumigWarn.sort(function(a,b){return a.jours-b.jours;});
    var fw=fumigWarn[0];
    alert.classList.add('show');
    document.getElementById('fumigTitle').textContent='🦟 Fumigation dans '+fw.jours+' jour'+(fw.jours>1?'s':'');
    document.getElementById('fumigSub').innerHTML='<strong>'+esc(fw.p.activite)+'</strong> prévue le <strong>'+fw.p.date+'</strong>.'
      +(fw.jours<=2?' <span style="color:var(--red);font-weight:700">— PRÉPARATION URGENTE</span>':'');
  } else alert.classList.remove('show');
}
function toggleNotif(){ document.getElementById('notifPanel').classList.toggle('open'); }
document.addEventListener('click',function(e){
  var wrap=document.getElementById('notifWrap');
  if(wrap&&!wrap.contains(e.target)) document.getElementById('notifPanel').classList.remove('open');
});

// ══ HELPERS ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
function mkChart(id,type,labels,datasets,opts){
  if(charts[id]) charts[id].destroy();
  try{ charts[id]=new Chart(document.getElementById(id),{type:type,data:{labels:labels,datasets:datasets},options:opts||BASE}); }catch(e){}
}
// ══ ANALYSE DES RISQUES (registre EvRP — fichier source) ══════
// Charge à la demande l'analyse ligne par ligne via le backend
// (getRiskAnalysisForClient) puis met en cache dans _riskData.
var _riskData=null, _riskLoading=false;
var RISK_SOURCE_URL='https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1_xbWzaV6HwT941mq_cvTjmH71QiM701haIa3fU-j3o0/edit?gid=1546767603';
function openRiskSource(){ openCleaningEmbed(RISK_SOURCE_URL,'Évaluation des risques — fichier source','CLASSEUR SOURCE','📊'); }
function renderRisk(){
  if(_riskData){ _renderRiskAll(); return; }
  if(_riskLoading) return;
  _riskLoading=true;
  var sum=document.getElementById('riskSum');
  if(sum) sum.innerHTML='⏳ Chargement de l\'analyse des risques (registre EvRP)…';
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(res){
      _riskLoading=false;
      if(!res||!res.ok){ if(sum) sum.innerHTML='⚠️ '+esc((res&&res.error)||'Erreur de chargement.'); return; }
      _riskData=res; _renderRiskAll();
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(err){
      _riskLoading=false;
      if(sum) sum.innerHTML='⚠️ Erreur réseau : '+esc((err&&err.message)||String(err));
    })
    .getRiskAnalysisForClient();
}

function _renderRiskAll(){
  var d=_riskData; if(!d) return;
  var N=d.total, k=d.kpis;
  var pctAcc=N?Math.round(d.avant[0]/N*100):0;
  var kp=document.getElementById('riskKpi');
  if(kp) kp.innerHTML=[
    kpiCard('Évaluations',N,'b','lignes du registre','k-b',null,null),
    kpiCard('Prioritaires',k.prioAvant,'r','Très Fort (avant)','k-r',N?Math.round(k.prioAvant/N*100):0,C.red),
    kpiCard('Prioritaires après',k.prioApres,'g','après actions','k-g',100,C.green),
    kpiCard('À traiter',k.sigAvant,'a','≥ Significatif','k-a',N?Math.round(k.sigAvant/N*100):0,C.amber),
    kpiCard('Score moyen',k.avgAvant+' → '+k.avgApres,'g','avant → après','k-g',null,null)
  ].join('');

  var sum=document.getElementById('riskSum');
  if(sum) sum.innerHTML='🛡️ <strong>'+N+'</strong> évaluations · Acceptable <strong style="color:#10c985">'+pctAcc+'%</strong>'
    +' · prioritaires (Très Fort) <strong style="color:#e8445a">'+k.prioAvant+'</strong> → <strong style="color:#10c985">'+k.prioApres+'</strong> après actions'
    +' · score moyen <strong>'+k.avgAvant+'→'+k.avgApres+'</strong> · source : onglet '+esc(d.sheet);

  var LV=['Acceptable','Marginal','Significatif','Très Fort','Inacceptable'];
  var LCOL=['#10c985','#f5a623','#f97316','#e8445a','#b3123a'];

  mkChart('riskLevelC','bar',LV,[
    {label:'Avant',data:d.avant,backgroundColor:'rgba(232,68,90,.78)',borderRadius:4},
    {label:'Après',data:d.apres,backgroundColor:'rgba(16,201,133,.78)',borderRadius:4}
  ],Object.assign({},BASE,{plugins:{legend:{display:true,labels:{color:C.txt,font:{size:10},boxWidth:10}}}}));

  mkChart('riskDoughC','doughnut',LV,[{data:d.avant,backgroundColor:LCOL,borderWidth:0,hoverOffset:4}],
    {responsive:true,maintainAspectRatio:false,plugins:{legend:{display:true,position:'right',labels:{color:C.txt,font:{size:9},boxWidth:9}}},cutout:'55%'});

  var hbar=Object.assign({},BASE,{indexAxis:'y',scales:{x:{grid:{color:C.grid},ticks:{color:C.txt}},y:{grid:{display:false},ticks:{color:C.txt,font:{size:9}}}}});
  function barFrom(id,arr,color){
    if(!arr) return;
    var labels=arr.map(function(x){return x.name.length>26?x.name.substring(0,26)+'…':x.name;});
    mkChart(id,'bar',labels,[{data:arr.map(function(x){return x.count;}),backgroundColor:color,borderRadius:4}],hbar);
  }
  barFrom('riskFamC', d.familles, 'rgba(13,168,210,.8)');
  barFrom('riskTypeC', d.risques, 'rgba(245,166,35,.85)');
  barFrom('riskLieuC', d.lieux, 'rgba(139,92,246,.8)');
  barFrom('riskDangC', d.dangers, 'rgba(20,184,166,.85)');

  // Par ligne de production (col Local) — barres empilées + table
  var lg=d.lignes||[];
  var lglabels=lg.map(function(x){return x.name.length>30?x.name.substring(0,30)+'…':x.name;});
  mkChart('riskLigneC','bar',lglabels,[
    {label:'Acceptable',data:lg.map(function(x){return x.niv[0];}),backgroundColor:'#10c985'},
    {label:'Marginal',data:lg.map(function(x){return x.niv[1];}),backgroundColor:'#f5a623'},
    {label:'Significatif',data:lg.map(function(x){return x.niv[2];}),backgroundColor:'#f97316'},
    {label:'Très Fort',data:lg.map(function(x){return x.niv[3];}),backgroundColor:'#e8445a'},
    {label:'Inacceptable',data:lg.map(function(x){return x.niv[4];}),backgroundColor:'#b3123a'}
  ],Object.assign({},BASE,{indexAxis:'y',plugins:{legend:{display:true,labels:{color:C.txt,font:{size:9},boxWidth:9}}},scales:{x:{stacked:true,grid:{color:C.grid},ticks:{color:C.txt}},y:{stacked:true,grid:{display:false},ticks:{color:C.txt,font:{size:9}}}}}));
  var hh='';
  lg.forEach(function(x){
    hh+='<tr><td style="font-weight:600">'+esc(x.name)+'</td><td style="text-align:center;font-weight:700">'+x.total+'</td>'
      +'<td style="text-align:center">'+x.niv[0]+'</td><td style="text-align:center">'+x.niv[1]+'</td><td style="text-align:center">'+x.niv[2]+'</td>'
      +'<td style="text-align:center;color:'+(x.niv[3]?'#e8445a':'var(--text3)')+';font-weight:'+(x.niv[3]?'700':'400')+'">'+x.niv[3]+'</td>'
      +'<td style="text-align:center;color:'+(x.prio?'#e8445a':'var(--text3)')+';font-weight:700">'+x.prio+'</td>'
      +'<td style="text-align:center">'+x.avg+'</td></tr>';
  });
  var lb=document.getElementById('riskLigneBody'); if(lb) lb.innerHTML=hh;

  _renderRiskMatrix();
  renderRiskLines();
}

function _renderRiskMatrix(){
  var d=_riskData, mx=d&&d.matrix; if(!mx) return;
  var maxc=1;
  mx.F.forEach(function(f){ mx.G.forEach(function(g){ var v=mx.cells[f+'x'+g]||0; if(v>maxc)maxc=v; }); });
  var h='<table style="border-collapse:collapse;font-size:11px;width:100%;text-align:center;min-width:380px">';
  h+='<thead><tr><th style="padding:6px;color:var(--text3)">Fréq. \\ Gravité</th>';
  mx.G.forEach(function(g){ h+='<th style="padding:6px;color:var(--text2)">'+g+'</th>'; });
  h+='<th style="padding:6px;color:var(--text2)">Total</th></tr></thead><tbody>';
  mx.F.forEach(function(f){
    h+='<tr><td style="padding:6px;font-weight:700;color:var(--p4)">'+f+'</td>';
    var tot=0;
    mx.G.forEach(function(g){
      var v=mx.cells[f+'x'+g]||0; tot+=v;
      var t=v/maxc, gg=Math.round(255-150*t);
      var bg=v?('rgb(255,'+gg+','+gg+')'):'transparent';
      h+='<td style="padding:6px;background:'+bg+';color:'+(t>0.55?'#fff':'var(--text2)')+';border:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,.06)">'+v+'</td>';
    });
    h+='<td style="padding:6px;font-weight:700">'+tot+'</td></tr>';
  });
  h+='<tr><td style="padding:6px;font-weight:700">Total</td>';
  var gt=0;
  mx.G.forEach(function(g){ var s=0; mx.F.forEach(function(f){ s+=mx.cells[f+'x'+g]||0; }); gt+=s; h+='<td style="padding:6px;font-weight:700">'+s+'</td>'; });
  h+='<td style="padding:6px;font-weight:700">'+gt+'</td></tr></tbody></table>';
  h+='<div style="font-size:9px;color:var(--text3);margin-top:6px">Fréquence : 2 = 1–5/mois … 5 = plusieurs/équipe · Gravité : 5 = soins bénins … 20 = accident mortel</div>';
  var box=document.getElementById('riskMatrix'); if(box) box.innerHTML=h;
}

function renderRiskLines(){
  var d=_riskData; if(!d) return;
  var fEl=document.getElementById('riskFilter');
  var q=((fEl&&fEl.value)||'').toLowerCase().trim();
  var rows=d.lines||[];
  if(q) rows=rows.filter(function(x){
    return (x.lieu+' '+x.zone+' '+x.tache+' '+x.danger+' '+x.risque+' '+x.fam+' '+x.dir+' '+x.serv).toLowerCase().indexOf(q)>-1;
  });
  var cnt=document.getElementById('riskLinesCount');
  if(cnt) cnt.textContent=rows.length+' affichées · '+d.critCount+' critiques'+(d.critCount>(d.lines||[]).length?' (max '+(d.lines||[]).length+' chargées)':'');
  var CAP=300, show=rows.slice(0,CAP);
  var LVB={'1- Acceptable':'#10c985','2- Marginal':'#f5a623','3- Significatif':'#f97316','4- Très Fort':'#e8445a','5- Inacceptable':'#b3123a'};
  var h='';
  show.forEach(function(x){
    var bc=LVB[x.c0]||'var(--text3)', ac=LVB[x.c1]||'var(--text3)';
    h+='<tr><td>'+esc(x.num)+'</td><td>'+esc(x.dir)+'</td><td>'+esc(x.serv)+'</td><td>'+esc(x.lieu)+'</td>'
      +'<td>'+esc(x.zone)+'</td><td>'+esc(x.tache)+'</td><td>'+esc(x.danger)+'</td><td>'+esc(x.risque)+'</td>'
      +'<td style="font-size:9px">'+esc(x.fam)+'</td>'
      +'<td style="text-align:center">'+(x.F==null?'':x.F)+'</td><td style="text-align:center">'+(x.P==null?'':x.P)+'</td><td style="text-align:center">'+(x.G==null?'':x.G)+'</td>'
      +'<td style="text-align:center;font-weight:700">'+(x.s0==null?'':x.s0)+'</td>'
      +'<td><span style="color:'+bc+';font-weight:600">'+esc(x.c0)+'</span></td>'
      +'<td><span style="color:'+ac+';font-weight:600">'+esc(x.c1)+'</span></td></tr>';
  });
  if(show.length===0) h='<tr><td colspan="15" style="text-align:center;color:var(--text3);padding:18px">Aucune ligne pour ce filtre</td></tr>';
  else if(rows.length>CAP) h+='<tr><td colspan="15" style="text-align:center;color:var(--text3);padding:10px">… '+(rows.length-CAP)+' lignes supplémentaires — affinez le filtre</td></tr>';
  var tb=document.getElementById('riskBody'); if(tb) tb.innerHTML=h;
}

// ══ PLAN D'ACTIONS GLOBAL (classeur consolidé — fichier source) ══
// Charge à la demande le plan d'actions via getActionPlanForClient
// puis met en cache dans _actData. Données non modifiées : les statuts
// affichés sont ceux du classeur source.
var _actData=null, _actLoading=false;
var ACTIONS_SOURCE_URL='https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1SI9RssYHEIAJ2djA8wfX1aQyVIoIR7auylmzkJBZ1f4/edit?gid=1664347988';
var ACT_STATUT_COL={'Clôturé / Terminé':'#10c985','En cours':'#0da8d2','En retard':'#e8445a','Non démarré':'#f5a623','Non renseigné':'#7c8b99'};
function openActionsSource(){ openCleaningEmbed(ACTIONS_SOURCE_URL,'Plan d\'actions global — fichier source','CLASSEUR SOURCE','📋'); }
function renderActions(){
  if(_actData){ _renderActionsAll(); return; }
  if(_actLoading) return;
  _actLoading=true;
  var sum=document.getElementById('actSum');
  if(sum) sum.innerHTML='⏳ Chargement du plan d\'actions global…';
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(res){
      _actLoading=false;
      if(!res||!res.ok){ if(sum) sum.innerHTML='⚠️ '+esc((res&&res.error)||'Erreur de chargement.'); return; }
      _actData=res; _renderActionsAll();
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(err){
      _actLoading=false;
      if(sum) sum.innerHTML='⚠️ Erreur réseau : '+esc((err&&err.message)||String(err));
    })
    .getActionPlanForClient();
}
function _renderActionsAll(){
  var d=_actData; if(!d) return;
  var N=d.total, k=d.kpis;
  var kp=document.getElementById('actKpi');
  if(kp) kp.innerHTML=[
    kpiCard('Actions',N,'b','plan d\'actions global','k-b',null,null),
    kpiCard('Clôturées',k.clot,'g','terminées','k-g',k.tauxClot,C.green),
    kpiCard('En cours',k.enCours,'b','en traitement','k-b',null,null),
    kpiCard('En retard',k.enRetard,'r','échéance dépassée','k-r',k.enRetardPct,C.red),
    kpiCard('Priorité élevée',k.prioElevee,'a','High / Gravité 3','k-a',null,null)
  ].join('');

  var sum=document.getElementById('actSum');
  if(sum) sum.innerHTML='📋 <strong>'+N+'</strong> actions · clôturées <strong style="color:#10c985">'+k.tauxClot+'%</strong> ('+k.clot+')'
    +' · en cours <strong style="color:#0da8d2">'+k.enCours+'</strong> · en retard <strong style="color:#e8445a">'+k.enRetard+'</strong>'
    +' · non démarrées <strong style="color:#f5a623">'+k.nonDemarre+'</strong> · source : onglet '+esc(d.sheet);

  var scol=d.statutOrder.map(function(s){return ACT_STATUT_COL[s]||'#7c8b99';});
  mkChart('actStatutC','doughnut',d.statutOrder,[{data:d.statutCounts,backgroundColor:scol,borderWidth:0,hoverOffset:4}],
    {responsive:true,maintainAspectRatio:false,plugins:{legend:{display:true,position:'right',labels:{color:C.txt,font:{size:9},boxWidth:9}}},cutout:'55%'});

  var bs=d.bySource||[];
  var blabels=bs.map(function(x){return x.name.length>24?x.name.substring(0,24)+'…':x.name;});
  mkChart('actSourceC','bar',blabels, d.statutOrder.map(function(s,ix){
    return {label:s,data:bs.map(function(x){return x.niv[ix];}),backgroundColor:ACT_STATUT_COL[s]||'#7c8b99'};
  }), Object.assign({},BASE,{indexAxis:'y',plugins:{legend:{display:true,labels:{color:C.txt,font:{size:8},boxWidth:8}}},scales:{x:{stacked:true,grid:{color:C.grid},ticks:{color:C.txt}},y:{stacked:true,grid:{display:false},ticks:{color:C.txt,font:{size:9}}}}}));

  var hbar=Object.assign({},BASE,{indexAxis:'y',scales:{x:{grid:{color:C.grid},ticks:{color:C.txt}},y:{grid:{display:false},ticks:{color:C.txt,font:{size:9}}}}});
  function barFrom(id,arr,color){
    if(!arr) return;
    var labels=arr.map(function(x){return x.name.length>26?x.name.substring(0,26)+'…':x.name;});
    mkChart(id,'bar',labels,[{data:arr.map(function(x){return x.count;}),backgroundColor:color,borderRadius:4}],hbar);
  }
  barFrom('actRespC', d.responsables, 'rgba(13,168,210,.8)');
  barFrom('actSiteC', d.sites, 'rgba(139,92,246,.8)');
  barFrom('actCatC', d.categories, 'rgba(245,166,35,.85)');

  var pcol=['#e8445a','#f5a623','#10c985','#7c8b99'];
  mkChart('actPrioC','bar',d.prioOrder,[{data:d.prioCounts,backgroundColor:pcol,borderRadius:4}],BASE);

  var fs=document.getElementById('actFStatut');
  if(fs && fs.options.length<=1) d.statutOrder.forEach(function(s){ var o=document.createElement('option'); o.value=s; o.textContent=s; fs.appendChild(o); });
  var fsrc=document.getElementById('actFSource');
  if(fsrc && fsrc.options.length<=1) bs.forEach(function(x){ var o=document.createElement('option'); o.value=x.name; o.textContent=x.name; fsrc.appendChild(o); });
  renderActionsTable();
}
function renderActionsTable(){
  var d=_actData; if(!d) return;
  var q=((document.getElementById('actFilter')||{}).value||'').toLowerCase().trim();
  var fst=(document.getElementById('actFStatut')||{}).value||'';
  var fsr=(document.getElementById('actFSource')||{}).value||'';
  var rows=(d.entries||[]).filter(function(x){
    if(fst && x.statut!==fst) return false;
    if(fsr && x.source!==fsr) return false;
    if(q && (x.id+' '+x.source+' '+x.site+' '+x.cat+' '+x.desc+' '+x.action+' '+x.resp+' '+x.prioRaw+' '+x.statut).toLowerCase().indexOf(q)===-1) return false;
    return true;
  });
  var cnt=document.getElementById('actCount'); if(cnt) cnt.textContent=rows.length+' / '+d.total+' actions';
  var CAP=400, show=rows.slice(0,CAP);
  var h='';
  show.forEach(function(x){
    var sc=ACT_STATUT_COL[x.statut]||'var(--text3)';
    h+='<tr><td>'+esc(x.id)+'</td><td style="font-size:9px">'+esc(x.source)+'</td><td>'+esc(x.site)+'</td>'
      +'<td style="font-size:9px">'+esc(x.cat)+'</td><td>'+esc(x.desc)+'</td><td>'+esc(x.action)+'</td>'
      +'<td>'+esc(x.resp)+'</td><td style="text-align:center">'+esc(x.prioRaw)+'</td>'
      +'<td style="text-align:center;font-size:9px;white-space:nowrap">'+esc(x.dCrea)+'</td>'
      +'<td style="text-align:center;font-size:9px;white-space:nowrap">'+esc(x.dEch)+'</td>'
      +'<td style="text-align:center;font-size:9px;white-space:nowrap">'+esc(x.dClot)+'</td>'
      +'<td><span style="color:'+sc+';font-weight:600;white-space:nowrap">'+esc(x.statut)+'</span></td></tr>';
  });
  if(show.length===0) h='<tr><td colspan="12" style="text-align:center;color:var(--text3);padding:18px">Aucune action pour ce filtre</td></tr>';
  else if(rows.length>CAP) h+='<tr><td colspan="12" style="text-align:center;color:var(--text3);padding:10px">… '+(rows.length-CAP)+' actions supplémentaires — affinez le filtre</td></tr>';
  var tb=document.getElementById('actBody'); if(tb) tb.innerHTML=h;
}
function kpiCard(lbl,val,color,sub,cls,pct,bc){
  var bar='';
  var dv=(typeof val==='number')?fmtNum(val):val;
  if(pct!=null){ bar='<div class="kpi-bar"><div class="kpi-bar-fill" style="width:'+Math.min(pct,100)+'%;background:'+bc+'"></div></div><div class="kpi-pct" style="color:'+bc+'">'+fmtNum(Math.min(pct,100))+'% obj.</div>'; }
  return'<div class="kpi '+cls+'"><div class="kpi-lbl">'+lbl+'</div><div class="kpi-val '+color+'">'+dv+'</div><div class="kpi-sub">'+sub+'</div>'+bar+'</div>';
}
function prog(lbl,val,tgt,lower,isPct){
  if(val===null||val===undefined) return'';
  if(!tgt||tgt===0) tgt=1;
  var pct=Math.min(Math.round(Math.abs(val)/Math.abs(tgt)*100),100);
  var ok=lower?val<=tgt:val>=tgt;
  var tc=ok?'ok':(pct>60?'warn':'bad'), bc=ok?'bg':(pct>60?'ba':'br');
  return'<div class="prow"><div class="phdr"><span class="plbl">'+lbl+'</span><span class="pnum '+tc+'">'+(isPct?fmtNum(val)+'%':fmtNum(val))+'</span></div><div class="pbg"><div class="pb '+bc+'" style="width:'+pct+'%"></div></div></div>';
}
function cleanMd(t){ if(!t||t==='null')return''; return t.replace(/\*\*/g,'').replace(/\*/g,'').replace(/#+\s*/g,'').replace(/\\n/g,'\n').replace(/\\-/g,'-').trim(); }
function cleanMonths(arr,hdrs){
  var lbs=[],dat=[];
  for(var i=0;i<Math.min((arr||[]).length,12);i++){
    if(arr[i]!==null&&arr[i]!==undefined){
      lbs.push(hdrs&&hdrs[i]?hdrs[i].replace(/-\d{2,4}$/,'').trim():ML[i]);
      dat.push(arr[i]);
    }
  }
  return{labels:lbs,data:dat};
}
function infoItem(lbl,val){ return val&&String(val).trim()&&val!=='—'?'<div class="info-item"><div class="info-lbl">'+lbl+'</div><div class="info-val">'+esc(String(val))+'</div></div>':''; }
function infoItemF(lbl,val){ return'<div class="info-item"><div class="info-lbl">'+lbl+'</div><div class="info-val">'+(val?esc(String(val)):'—')+'</div></div>'; }
function esc(s){ return String(s||'').replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;'); }
function escAttr(s){ return String(s||'').replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/"/g,'&quot;').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;'); }
function fmtNum(v){
  if(v===null||v===undefined||v==='') return v;
  var n=parseFloat(v); if(isNaN(n)) return v;
  var s=n.toFixed(2); return s.replace(/\.00$/,'');
}

// ══ MODES ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function setMode(m){
  viewMode=m;
  document.getElementById('btnYtd').classList.toggle('on',m==='ytd');
  document.getElementById('btnMois').classList.toggle('on',m==='mois');
  if(D){updateC1();updateC2();}
}
function setPyrMode(m){
  pyrMode=m;
  document.getElementById('pyrYB').classList.toggle('on',m==='ytd');
  document.getElementById('pyrMB').classList.toggle('on',m==='mois');
  document.getElementById('pyrSel').style.display=m==='mois'?'inline-block':'none';
  renderPyramid();
}

// ══ PYRAMIDE ══════════════════════════════════════════════════
function getCSSVar(name){ return getComputedStyle(document.documentElement).getPropertyValue(name).trim(); }
function populatePyrMonths(){
  var sel=document.getElementById('pyrSel');
  if(!sel||!D) return;
  var m=D.metrics, hdrs=D.monthHeaders||[];
  var aMj=m.atM_months||[], aMn=m.atm_months||[], aI=m.inc_months||[], aT=m.tags_months||[];
  var n=Math.max(hdrs.length, aMj.length, aMn.length, aI.length, aT.length, 12);
  var prev=sel.value;
  var opts='', firstVal=null, lastVal=null, hasPrev=false;
  for(var i=0;i<n;i++){
    var hasData=(aMj[i]!=null)||(aMn[i]!=null)||(aI[i]!=null)||(aT[i]!=null);
    if(!hasData) continue;
    var lbl=(hdrs[i]?String(hdrs[i]).replace(/-\d{2,4}$/,'').trim():'')||ML[i]||('M'+(i+1));
    var v=String(i);
    opts+='<option value="'+v+'">'+esc(lbl)+'</option>';
    if(firstVal===null) firstVal=v;
    lastVal=v;
    if(v===prev) hasPrev=true;
  }
  sel.innerHTML=opts;
  if(hasPrev) sel.value=prev;
  else if(lastVal!==null) sel.value=lastVal;
}
function renderPyramid(){
  if(!D) return;
  var m=D.metrics;
  populatePyrMonths();
  var sel=document.getElementById('pyrSel');
  var fatal,majeur,mineur,incident,tags;
  if(pyrMode==='ytd'){ fatal=m.at_fatal;majeur=m.at_majeur;mineur=m.at_mineur;incident=m.inc_ytd;tags=m.tags_ytd; }
  else{
